EIA DUC Report

January 22, 2018 in Drilled and Completed, DUCs
Overview of EIA DUC Inventory Report A drilled but uncompleted well (DUC) is a new well after the end of the drilling process, but its first completion process has not been concluded. EIA uses 20 days to estimate days to TD. This likely overestimates DUC inventory in basins where PAD drilling is predominant. Report tracks monthly changes in DUC inventory beginning in 2014. Permian Monthly Highlights Permian Basin ended December with ~2,777 wells waiting on completion.

Limelight: A Closer Look at Diamondback's New Position

 Feb 2, 2018
Focus Diamondback recently announced a new exploration play targeting the Mississippian oil play in Ector and Crane Counties. Company acquired ~19,000 acres which they plan on delineating beginning this year. The map below identifies offsetting permit/spud activity. Majority of activity is vertical development, with the most active operator, Oxy, North of their acreage. Adventure Operating has completed 2 horizontal wells on their acreage in 2016 and 2017 targeting the San Andreas formation.

EIA DUC Report

 Feb 2, 2018
Overview of EIA DUC Inventory Report A drilled but uncompleted well (DUC) is a new well after the end of the drilling process, but its first completion process has not been concluded. EIA uses 20 days to estimate days to TD. This likely overestimates DUC inventory in basins where PAD drilling is predominant. Report tracks monthly changes in DUC inventory beginning in 2014. Permian Monthly Highlights Permian Basin ended December with ~2,880 wells waiting on completion.

Oil and Gas Producer Pricing Index

 Feb 2, 2018
Producer Pricing Index What does it measure? The Producer Price Index (PPI) program measures the average change over time in the selling prices received by domestic producers for their output. The prices included in the PPI are from the first commercial transaction for many products and some services. Why is it useful? Commonly used in escalating purchase and sales contracts. Indicator of overall price movement at the producer level.

Permian Basin Peer 2018 Production and Hedging Estimates

 Feb 2, 2018
Methodology and Focus Sourced data from a combination of investor presentations, quarterly reports and FactSet. Summarize company hedging profiles for Permian Basin operators. Identify which companies are at risk from price inflation or deflation. Determine oil production estimates for 2018. Highlights Of the companies which produce more than 100 MBbls/d, only Pioneer and Concho have hedged more than 50% of 2018 production. Parsley stands out with ~100% of 2018 oil hedged.
